# Risklayer Spreadsheet Download

Because of high access rates to the Google Spreadsheet of Risklayer, access has been limited.
You can download the latest spreadsheet as a .xlsx file from our API.
We update this file every 30 minutes at xx:00 and xx:30.

The .xlsx file is not modified from our side and uses the google export to .xlsx function.

Please use the following URL: https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/cases-risklayer/xlsx

> The timestamp in the filename is UTC-based.

If you only want to check the timestamp of the file, use: https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/cases-risklayer/xlsx-last-update

Example output:
```json
{
  "last_update": "2021-04-19T20-05-33Z"
}
```

> Checkout the API docs: https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/apidocs


## CoronaVis API

If you only need the case numbers and deaths, you may also access our API directly.

Our endpoints return GeoJSON.

There are two schematic endpoints.

### All regions

To get all regions from a certain aggregation level use:

```
https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/cases-risklayer/development/<landkreise|regierungsbezirke|bundeslaender|laender>?from=2020-01-01&to=2020-04-20&nogeom=true
```

The query parameters are optional.
The returned FeatureCollection (GeoJSON) will contain the shapes of the regions as well as the properties where the statistics is available per day.

Example:

```
https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/cases-risklayer/development/bundeslaender?from=2020-04-15&to=2020-04-20
```

### Specific region

For a specific region the schema looks like this:

```
https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/cases-risklayer/development/<landkreis|regierungsbezirk|bundesland|land>/<AGS>?from=2020-01-01&to=2020-04-20&nogeom=true
```

The AGS refers to the [Common Identification Number for Germany](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community_Identification_Number#Germany).
For Konstanz this is for example *08335* and Baden-Württemberg it is *08*.

The query parameters are again optional.

An example call may look like this:

```
https://api.coronavis.dbvis.de/cases-risklayer/development/landkreis/08335?from=2020-04-15&to=2020-04-20
```
